method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)

  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;

  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    assert pcount == CountPositive(a[..i]); // added assertion
    assert ncount == CountNegative(a[..i]); // added assertion

      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

  (x > 0 && d > 0) || (x < 0 && d < 0)
}

ghost function CountPositiveAfterDiv(a: seq<int>, d: int): int
  requires d != 0
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountPositiveAfterDiv(a[..|a|-1], d)
       + (if IsPositiveAfterDiv(a[|a|-1], d) then 1 else 0)
}

ghost function CeilHalf(n: int): int
{
  (n + 1) / 2
}

ghost function CountPositive(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountPositive(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] > 0 then 1 else 0)
}

ghost function CountNegative(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountNegative(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] < 0 then 1 else 0)
}

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert pcount == CountPositive(a);
  assert ncount == CountNegative(a);
  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    foreach d' in {x | x != 0} 
      assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountNegative(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] < 0 then 1 else 0)
}

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    assert d > 0;
    CountPosDivPos(a, d);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    assert d < 0;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, d);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    // postcondition: d != 0
    assert d != 0;
    // CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a);
    // CountPositive(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|) because pcount >= half
    assert CountPositive(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|);
    // combine to get required postcondition
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    // postcondition: d != 0
    assert d != 0;
    // CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a);
    // CountNegative(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|) because ncount >= half
    assert CountNegative(a) >= CeilHalf(|a|);
    // combine to get required postcondition
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    // d == 0
    assert d == 0;
    // ensure that for all nonzero d', CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    forall d' :: d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        // CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountPositive(a)
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountPositive(a);
        // CountPositive(a) < CeilHalf(|a|) by earlier condition
        assert CountPositive(a) < CeilHalf(|a|);
      } else {
        // CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountNegative(a)

        // CountNegative(a) < CeilHalf(|a|) by earlier condition
        assert CountNegative(a) < CeilHalf(|a|);
      }
    }
  }

  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000

  var ncount := 0;

    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {

      pcount := pcount + 1;

  requires d != 0
{
  (x > 0 && d > 0) || (x < 0 && d < 0)
}

ghost function CountPositiveAfterDiv(a: seq<int>, d: int): int
  requires d != 0
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountPositiveAfterDiv(a[..|a|-1], d)
       + (if IsPositiveAfterDiv(a[|a|-1], d) then 1 else 0)
}

ghost function CeilHalf(n: int): int
{
  (n + 1) / 2
}

ghost function CountPositive(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountPositive(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] > 0 then 1 else 0)
}

ghost function CountNegative(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountNegative(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] < 0 then 1 else 0)
}

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}
